    def removeAtHead(self):
    
        """Remove node at head end."""
    
        if self.__size == 0:
            return None
        elif self.__size == 1:
            nodeToRemove = self.__head.next
            self.__sentinel.next = None
            nodeToRemove.prev = None
            self.__size -= 1
            return nodeToRemove
        else:

            nextNode = nodeToRemove.next
            self.__sentinel.next = nextNode
